[1;37r[34;1H[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# This boolean parameter controls whether Samba attempts to sync the Unix[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# password with the SMB password when the encrypted SMB password in the[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d

[1;37r[34;1H[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# For Unix password sync to work on a Debian GNU/Linux system, the following[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# parameters must be set (thanks to Ian Kahan <<kahan@informatik.tu-muenchen.de> for[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# sending the correct chat script for the passwd program in Debian Sarge).[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;4Hpasswd program = /usr/bin/passwd %u[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;4Hpasswd chat = *Enter\snew\s*\spassword:* %n\n *Retype\snew\s*\spassword:* %n\n *password\supdate[0;10;7m>[34;1H[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# This boolean controls whether PAM will be used for password changes[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# when requested by an SMB client instead of the program listed in[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# 'passwd program'. The default is 'no'.[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d

[1;37r[34;1H[36m# to anonymous connections[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d

[1;37r[34;1H[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# It specifies the location of the user's[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# profile directory from the client point of view) The following[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# required a [profiles] share to be setup on the samba server (see[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d

[1;37r[34;1H[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# The following setting only takes effect if 'domain logons' is set[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d

[1;37r[34;1H[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# The following setting only takes effect if 'domain logons' is set[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H[36m# It specifies the script to run during logon. The script must be stored[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d

[1;37r[34;1H; add user script = /usr/sbin/adduser --quiet --disabled-password --gecos "" %u[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d

[1;37r[34;1H[36m# This allows machine accounts to be created on the domain controller via the [39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d

[1;37r[34;1H[36m# The following assumes a "machines" group exists on the system[39m[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
[1;37r[34;1H; add machine script  = /usr/sbin/useradd -g machines -c "%u machine account" -d /var/lib/samba -s [0;10;7m>[34;1H[m[?25l[?1c[?25h[?0c7[2;35r8[35d
